Dear Jay,
Thank you for your emails and the amended offer. We accept the updated quotation.
1. Documentation
Attached are high-resolution photos showing the engraved serial numbers K08059-43 and K08059-48 on both reactors.
We are updating the CIPL and Commercial Invoice to include these serial numbers and the exact clause:
“Temporary Export for Repair and Return – No transfer of ownership. Goods will be returned to UAE after completion of repair.”
2. Schedule
Pickup from Mirfa is tentatively scheduled for 25 February 2026, subject to final site readiness and possible change.
We confirm the trailer configuration exactly as proposed: 1 x Special Low Bed (Mirfa collection) and 1 x Low Bed + 1 x Flat Bed (transit with transloading in your yard).
3. Clearance Requirements
To ensure smooth temporary export and zero-duty re-import, please confirm DSV’s full responsibilities and advise on document preparation as follows:
UAE side: Will DSV handle Temporary Export Declaration, Exit/Entry Certificate, and Bond/Guarantee?
KSA side: Will DSV coordinate with the consignee’s Batha clearing agent (details to be provided by 20 February), FASAH pre-declaration (48h prior), and SABER/SASO exemption for HS 8504 reactors?
Please provide the complete list of required documents and clearly indicate:
What DSV will prepare/handle,
What we must prepare (including attested Certificate of Origin, Arabic translations, and Chamber attestation where required for this temporary repair movement).
Please also update us on the 3rd-party KSA transport rate.
Kindly send your detailed confirmation by 20 February 2026 so we can lock the window and proceed. Let us know if any further documents are required from our side.

Best regards,
Minkyu Cha
